Subject: This week's concert report, and a Cat Power ticket giveaway...
Body:  Cat's Cradle<https://cdn.ticketfly.com/i/00/00/57/08/63-ethm.jpg> 


Another huge week of concerts is upon us! See below for details on one
of our biggest weeks of the year.

BIRDSMELL RESCHEDULED:
Birdsmell (aka Ben Bridwell from Band Of Horses) was forced to cancel
last week after losing his voice. Fortunately, he was able to quickly
reschedule! He'll be at Cat's Cradle's Back Room TONIGHT, 11/5.

WIN CAT POWER TICKETS!
Cat Power will play a special solo show at Cat's Cradle 11/10 and we're
giving away a pair of tickets! To enter, just send an email to
mailer@catscradle.com with subject line POWER. We'll notify the winner,
who will be randomly drawn, by 11/8. GOOD LUCK!

Another huge week of concerts is upon us! See below for details on one
of our biggest weeks of the year.

BIRDSMELL RESCHEDULED:
Birdsmell (aka Ben Bridwell from Band Of Horses) was forced to cancel
last week after losing his voice. Fortunately, he was able to quickly
reschedule! He'll be at Cat's Cradle's Back Room TONIGHT, 11/5.

WIN CAT POWER TICKETS!
Cat Power will play a special solo show at Cat's Cradle 11/10 and we're
giving away a pair of tickets! To enter, just send an email to
mailer@catscradle.com with subject line POWER. We'll notify the winner,
who will be randomly drawn, by 11/8. GOOD LUCK!

Another huge week of concerts is upon us! See below for details on one
of our biggest weeks of the year.

BIRDSMELL RESCHEDULED:
Birdsmell (aka Ben Bridwell from Band Of Horses) was forced to cancel
last week after losing his voice. Fortunately, he was able to quickly
reschedule! He'll be at Cat's Cradle's Back Room TONIGHT, 11/5.

WIN CAT POWER TICKETS!
Cat Power will play a special solo show at Cat's Cradle 11/10 and we're
giving away a pair of tickets! To enter, just send an email to
mailer@catscradle.com with subject line POWER. We'll notify the winner,
who will be randomly drawn, by 11/8. GOOD LUCK!

Another huge week of concerts is upon us! See below for details on one
of our biggest weeks of the year.

BIRDSMELL RESCHEDULED:
Birdsmell (aka Ben Bridwell from Band Of Horses) was forced to cancel
last week after losing his voice. Fortunately, he was able to quickly
reschedule! He'll be at Cat's Cradle's Back Room TONIGHT, 11/5.

WIN CAT POWER TICKETS!
Cat Power will play a special solo show at Cat's Cradle 11/10 and we're
giving away a pair of tickets! To enter, just send an email to
mailer@catscradle.com with subject line POWER. We'll notify the winner,
who will be randomly drawn, by 11/8. GOOD LUCK!
